102011440397064732199< /UserId.>
< Text>
This spot speaks for itself. From the beautiful views of the Bay Bridge to the ample seating they provide outside.

The staff is very friendly and always willing to let you try the beers before you commit.

From Freezie Pop to Local Honey, Woods beer offers a wide variety of choices for very beer lovers palate.

Nestled in the very cozy area of Treasure Island, this place is a treasure in itself that caters to the beer lovers taste, and also offers empanadas!

Delicious, flaky South American style pastries that are hot and full of delicious ingredients that vary from beef to ham and cheese!< /Text>

<Review>Nestled right between the 110/101 freeways as well as Dodger Stadium + Downtown LA, this location is a fairly convenient stopping point especially since it has its own parking lot + self-checkout stations for when there's a long line. And yes, fairly frequently there is a line of at least 5 customers despite 2-3 employees working the registers.

I only come to this particular CVS location on Sunset due to its proximity to my stomping grounds. It's just your typical 24-hour CVS where you can get all your basic toiletries, stationary, makeup, snacks, holiday cards, alcohol, medication, etc at any time of day or night. The photo station is right next to the cash registers, + the pharmacy is in the back. They tend to be pretty good about keeping things pretty well-stocked so I've never had a problem finding anything even if it's on sale in the weekly ads.

The 3-stars is a stamp of mediocrity. < Text>
We came in August and the beach was virtually empty! It‚Äôs cold and foggy in the mornings so the water is freezing and never warmed up. But we had a blast and got to watch a large pod of dolphins hunting super near the shore for an hour or so. Lots of kelp and tiny sea shells, some sea glass and the occasional crab. There is plenty of sand, some picnic benches, extra bathrooms and the park itself is lovely, although it did get crowded with parents and little ones too young for school just before lunchtime. It‚Äôs a large play structure/area and not really a problem. This really is an underrated spot!< /Text>

<Text>The boba/tea standards in the bay area are high, and Milpitas already had a high concentration of boba tea shops before Tea Top opened up a few years ago. I will have to say though that they've definitely come to become a strong standard in the area with quality teas, great boba, and a good consistency with their product and customer service regardless of when you go in.

The only thing I would change about them would be to wish that their venue space seemed more inviting for hanging out. I really enjoy the atmosphere of Factory Tea Bar in Fremont; makes you want to meet up with friends there. The atmosphere of Tea Top is clean, but just doesn't have the right modern vibe. But that's a pretty small impact factor; not enough for me to dock them off a star.

Quality, price, and consistency are the true winners here. I go to Tea Top and grab drinks to go because I know I'll get what I expect, and they'll craft the drinks quickly. (I-Tea can have ridiculously long waits these days.)<//Text>< Date>

< text>
Art Deco interiors are met with new age dining options - you can be a picky eater here. Lots of vegan and gluten free options/substitutes. I‚Äôve been coming here since 2007 and they always hit the spot.

The vibes in this cafe are on point. Colorful posters decorate the walls and there are neat circular windows along the walls.

Grab a menu (you‚Äôll see them) and seat yourself upon arrival. I always get something different, and I am always happy with it. From their Vegan nachos with cheese, guac and black beans to their breakfast with eggs, bacon and potatoes - all of it is good.

If you like sweets, look at the bar area to see slices of the cakes they have that day, kept in glass cake stands.

Perfect for solo dining or for parties of around 6.<//text>

< review>
Fantastic place. Great atmosphere and great food. Modern organic, vegan friendly take on a classic American diner.

We went in for breakfast and ended up have the chicken sandwich - it was sublime. My partner had it with the salad and a ranch dressing and I had it with fries. Even the fries were great. Cut straight from the potato and super fluffy.  A really good potion size. I seriously didn't think I would finish all the fries after the sandwich but I couldn't leave such yummy fries. Fresh chicken with bacon and avocado in a delicious brioche bun.

Service was quick and efficient and who ever the guy was at the front... despite his no nonsense attitude, I really enjoyed his attentiveness and accent.
Top place to go.</review>

<rate>4</rate><Review>A fixture of my own personal post-outing nightlife since way back when, Swingers is a staple of Santa Monica since long before the metro rail and Starbucks boom of the WestSide gentrification era. A amalgamation of omni, vegetarian, and vegan options keep the vast menu accessible to most if not all dining preferences, while the coffees, shakes, and sinful desserts offer a plethora of treats for those looking for less than a meal. Long hours, free wifi, and beautiful, quirky, and attentive servers maintain the venue's neighborhood cafe vibe, while sustaining that old-school Santa Monica community feel. A definite must see for anyone seeking a reminder of what L.A. used to be!</Review>< Pictures>
